19521615-11&cookie_name=utmrss&guid=on&utmn=3800321295',)":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn100@2020_3/2020/08/24/14-09-14-692_cf5aa6e6c1d837bc.jpg"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598278128952},{"createdTime":"2020-08-24 22:08:48","updatedTime":"2020-08-24 22:08:48","title":"说出来你可能不信，这些治病、减肥和救命的药，全都来自毒物","link":"https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/m4YwdS2k57sR5ezlLHwI-A","description":"<div>\n <div class=\"rich_media_content \" id=\"js_content\"> \n  <section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p><span>中世纪时，一种可怕的疾病忽然在欧洲各国间流行开来：患者或是经历光怪陆离的幻觉，导致丧失劳动能力，或是手足逐渐溃烂，直到肢体坏死而残疾 <span> [1] </span> 。 </span></p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n     <p><span>严重的病症给患者带来烈火焚身般的痛苦，那时人们以为这是神灵的惩罚，称其为“圣火” <span> （或“圣安东尼之火”） </span> 。 </span></p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <section> \n      <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n       <section>\n        <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.8514286\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"700\" src=\"https://2-im.guokr.com/1IpVQziv5qoJJyXy5wrlLl8Y10-lQ0I3kvTvBC2iDlm8AgAAVAIAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/472\" />\n       </section> \n      </section> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>1568年的一副画作，描述了“圣安东尼之火”的幸存者乞讨为生的悲惨生活 |&nbsp;Pieter Bruegel&nbsp;de Oude</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p><span>造成这种病症的罪魁祸首，其实是 <span> <strong> 麦角菌属 </strong> </span> <span> （ <em> Claviceps </em> ） </span> 的 <strong> <span> 真菌 </span> </strong> 。它会悄悄潜入小麦等禾本科植物的子房，长成一粒粒有毒的“麦角”，混入麦粒中，最后一同磨成面粉被人食用。 </span></p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <section> \n      <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n       <section>\n        <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"1.3032967\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"455\" src=\"https://1-im.guokr.com/ytG6EHp4MCzHHnBef-6k65o9i1eLwJf4VbZ28viZyIzHAQAAUQIAAFBO.png\" />\n       </section> \n      </section> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>黑麦麦角菌（ <em> Claviceps purpurea </em> ）的侵染过程 | Wikimedia Commons, <span> Franz Eugen Köhler, Köhler’s Medizinal-Pflanzen / Public Domain </span></p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p><span>麦角中含有生物碱，有的作用于神经系统，使人产生严重的幻觉和精神错乱，还有的作用于循环系统，让四肢的血管收缩，导致肢体失去血液供应而坏死。 <span> <strong> 所谓的“圣安东尼之火”，其实就是重症麦角中毒。 </strong> </span> </span></p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <section> \n      <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n       <section>\n        <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.75\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"1024\" src=\"https://2-im.guokr.com/NkbvrxafkBuh7fN5BgWfhS76pH_Ba7kSoFmpDrtsKAwABAAAAAMAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/416\" />\n       </section> \n      </section> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>混在麦粒中的麦角，就是“圣安东尼之火”的罪魁祸首 | Wikimedia Commons, <span> Dominique Jacquin / CC BY-SA <span> (https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by-sa/3.0) </span> </span></p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>所幸，随着农业技术的进步，麦角中毒事件已鲜有发生。不过，麦角并未就此退出人类的生活，而是以截然不同的另一种身份再度活跃起来。</p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n     <p>近年来， <span> <strong> 人们逐个分离出麦角中的活性生物碱，将其提纯或改造后应用于医疗领域 <span> [ </span> </strong> </span> <span> 2] </span> 。比如，麦角新碱可以促进子宫收缩，可以治疗产后大出血；麦角胺，被用于治疗严重的偏头痛；人工合成的卡麦角林和溴隐亭，则成了治疗帕金森病的良药……</p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <section> \n      <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n       <section> \n        <section>\n         <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"1.8163265\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"343\" src=\"https://2-im.guokr.com/0rUmYdsfQWZEIo5_77Z9TaibApM5vxufn1_F7WqXqP1XAQAAbwIAAFBO.png\" />\n        </section> \n       </section> \n      </section> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>麦角衍生物可有效阻止产后出血 | Wikimedia Commons, <span> Harmid / </span> <span> Public Domain </span></p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>麦角已华丽变身成为医学界的不可或缺的药物原料，而像这样转变角色的生物，远不止麦角。</p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <section> \n      <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n       <section> \n        <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n         <section> \n          <section> \n           <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n            <section> \n             <section> \n              <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n               <section> \n                <section> \n                 <section>\n                  <svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\"> \n                  </svg>\n                 </section> \n                </section> \n               </section> \n              </section> \n             </section> \n            </section> \n           </section> \n          </section> \n          <section> \n           <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n            <section> \n             <section> \n              <p><strong><span>源自毒蜥的降糖药 </span> </strong></p> \n             </section> \n            </section> \n           </section> \n          </section> \n          <section> \n           <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n            <section> \n             <section> \n              <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n               <section> \n                <section> \n                 <section>\n                  <svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\"> \n                  </svg>\n                 </section> \n                </section> \n               </section> \n              </section> \n             </section> \n            </section> \n           </section> \n          </section> \n         </section> \n        </section> \n       </section> \n      </section> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>在美国的部分区域， <span> <strong> 希拉毒蜥 </strong> </span> <span> （ <em> Heloderma suspectum </em> ） </span> 是人们唯恐避之不及的一种生物。它的下颌唾液中会分泌毒液，一旦被咬伤，会引起强烈剧痛、恶心呕吐，甚至患上严重的胰腺炎。</p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n     <p>然而，在这种毒蜥的身上，科学家们却发现了一类全新的药物， <span> <strong> 不仅可以帮助糖尿病患者控制血糖，还可用于治疗肥胖症。 </strong> </span></p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <section> \n      <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n       <section>\n        <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.6692708\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"768\" src=\"https://2-im.guokr.com/csHjwMfn4ic6eRHcviS4bVhspfFza2W2AGB9ftnXGsEAAwAAAgIAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/371\" />\n       </section> \n      </section> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>希拉毒蜥（ <em> Heloderma suspectum </em> ），是降糖药艾塞那肽的研发起点 |&nbsp;Wikimedia Commons, <span> H. van der Ploeg / CC BY-SA (https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by-sa/3.0) </span></p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>20世纪90年代，年轻的研究人员约翰·恩 <span> （John&nbsp;Eng） </span> 开始研究希拉毒蜥所分泌的唾液，并试图从其中寻找到有利用价值的化合物。</p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n     <p>他意外发现，希拉毒蜥唾液中存在的一种物质，能够降低实验鼠的血糖。仔细硏究后，他发现， <span> <strong> 这种物质和人体内已知的一种降糖激素——胰高血糖素样肽-1 </strong> </span> <span> （GLP-1） </span> <span> <strong> 具有相同作用 </strong> </span> <span> [3] </span> 。</p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n     <p>早在十多年前，科学家们就认识到了GLP-1的降糖作用，它可以根据人体当前血糖浓度，自动调节分泌胰岛素的速率。可惜的是，人体内自然产生的GLP-1激素十分脆弱，注进人体后不一会儿就会被降解而失去作用，这一点让它不适合被制成药物。</p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n     <p>而约翰·恩发现的这种物质在体内恰好不容易降解：能存留很长时间发挥作用。进一步的临床试验证明，这种药物只需每天注射两次，就可以有效帮助糖尿病患者控制血糖，效果比起口服降糖药丝毫不逊色。基于大型临床试验中的显著效果，这款名为Byetta <span> （艾塞那肽） </span> 的药物于2005年获FDA批准上市。</p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n     <p>在艾塞那肽上市之后，其他多种仿GLP-1激素药物也相继进入临床，其中就包括曾创下数十亿美元年销售记录的利拉鲁肽——这种药除了用于治疗糖尿病，还曾于2014年获批用于肥胖症的辅助治疗，能有效降低体重和减少肥胖症并发症 <span> [4] </span> 。</p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <section> \n      <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n       <section>\n        <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.7344173\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"369\" src=\"https://2-im.guokr.com/V1RW22Je_jI6wMwh4x1tj1PyDEBdec6QJn422zFdyLxxAQAADwEAAEpQ.jpg\" />\n       </section> \n      </section> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>利拉鲁肽是FDA批准的“减肥药”之一（此为处方药，可能有潜在副作用，需要在医生的指导下使用） | flickr, Doctor 4U / CC BY <span> (https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/2.0/ </span> <span> ) </span></p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <section> \n      <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n       <section> \n        <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n         <section> \n          <section> \n           <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n            <section> \n             <section> \n              <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n               <section> \n                <section> \n                 <section>\n                  <svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\"> \n                  </svg>\n                 </section> \n                </section> \n               </section> \n              </section> \n             </section> \n            </section> \n           </section> \n          </section> \n          <section> \n           <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n            <section> \n             <section> \n              <p><strong><span>从“蒙汗药”到“救命针” </span> </strong></p> \n             </section> \n            </section> \n           </section> \n          </section> \n          <section> \n           <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n            <section> \n             <section> \n              <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n               <section> \n                <section> \n                 <section>\n                  <svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\"> \n                  </svg>\n                 </section> \n                </section> \n               </section> \n              </section> \n             </section> \n            </section> \n           </section> \n          </section> \n         </section> \n        </section> \n       </section> \n      </section> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>作为一种古老的药用植物， <span> <strong> 曼陀罗 </strong> </span> 生来就集“毒药”和“神药”于一身。人类很早就开始用曼陀罗来医治疾病，或者对付仇人。从《本草纲目》里的麻醉药,到《水浒传》中的“蒙汗药”，都有曼陀罗的身影。</p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <section> \n      <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n       <section>\n        <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.75\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"1024\" src=\"https://2-im.guokr.com/RrAjhAR5fRMaMP4mU3SIN0koE-IuuDBJ3Ecki1ZwrMUABAAAAAMAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/416\" />\n       </section> \n      </section> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>曼陀罗蕴藏着毒性和不可低估的药用价值 |&nbsp;Wikimedia Commons, Skäpperöd / CC BY-SA <span> (https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by-sa/3.0) </span></p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>现代医学创立之后，曼陀罗的“毒药”角色渐渐淡出，它致人麻醉的原理也彻底揭开：曼陀罗中含有一种名为“东莨菪碱”的化学物质，可以干扰人体神经系统的重要信使——乙酰胆碱的功能，从而导致意识混乱、肌肉松弛、出汗减少、胃肠蠕动减缓等效应 <span> [5] </span> 。</p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n     <p>人们已经挖掘出曼陀罗中一些 <span> <strong> 生物碱 </strong> </span> <span> （尤其是东莨菪碱和阿托品） </span> 的医疗价值，它们现在被用于治疗多种疾病。</p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n     <p>例如，东莨菪碱长期被用来治疗肠道功能紊乱、内脏痉挛、晕车晕船等，而阿托品已经成为了抢救农药中毒、致命性心动过缓等危及生命情况的重要用药。在现代医院的抢救推车中，有一个位置就是留给阿托品的 <span> [6] </span> 。</p> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <section> \n      <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n       <section>\n        <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.9540373\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"805\" src=\"https://1-im.guokr.com/-rwTcWprRLDUXHDmylDn595DO5xJpQ2OSvl6H21sodslAwAAAAMAAEpQ.jpg?imageView2/1/w/555/h/529\" />\n       </section> \n      </section> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>阿托品已成为急救必备药品 | Wikimedia Commons, <span> Wesalius / CC BY (https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/4.0) </span></p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>自古以来，我们身边从来不乏各种毒物的身影，它们一度夺去了无数人的健康和生命。而今， <span> <strong> 许多原本令人唯恐避之不及的毒物，被药学家们赋予了全新的打开方式，摇身变成了救死扶伤的良药 </strong> </span> ，在人类历史中留下浓墨重彩的一笔。</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <section> \n      <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n       <section>\n        <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.0652174\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"690\" src=\"https://2-im.guokr.com/Eou_K6zHNGSFxqwwN1IRjF3AO2ugGBpKoe6OLB05TKuyAgAALQAAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/36\" />\n       </section> \n      </section> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n    <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n     <section> \n      <section>\n       <svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\"> \n       </svg>\n      </section> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n    <section 23-708_9a04708d4c16d72f.webp","https://2-im.guokr.com/Eou_K6zHNGSFxqwwN1IRjF3AO2ugGBpKoe6OLB05TKuyAgAALQAAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/36":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn4@2020_2/2020/08/24/14-09-13-250_8d765392fcbe4612.webp","https://3-im.guokr.com/RpQCwV4e4ufaMvMZYCwAvWqv_60REruf-Vb5VDlinZ-ZAwAAogEAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/251":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn15@2020_4/2020/08/24/14-09-22-327_9368367a929cae44.webp","https://3-im.guokr.com/fzyhzieBooVa-rMa89wlAilePavy-mqb52dyqhZp_is4BAAADgIAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/270":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn4@2020_4/2020/08/24/14-09-23-736_2fefb4389c16a9a0.webp","https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/('//analytics.guokr.com/ga.gif?utmp=https%3A%2F%2Fmp.weixin.qq.com%2Fs%2Fm4YwdS2k57sR5ezlLHwI-A&utmac=UA-19521615-11&cookie_name=utmrss&guid=on&utmn=173564244',)":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn36@2020_1/2020/08/24/14-09-23-609_0321634e53717587.jpg"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598278128955},{"createdTime":"2020-08-24 22:08:48","updatedTime":"2020-08-24 22:08:48","title":"今夜去看流星雨，落在这地球上","link":"https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/5abyFoVjCK1RaN025Tr0yA","description":"<div>\n <div class=\"rich_media_content \" id=\"js_content\"> \n  <section data-label=\"powered by xmt.cn\" data-tools=\"新媒体管家\">\n   &nbsp;\n  </section> \n  <section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section>\n     <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"1\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" src=\"https://3-im.guokr.com/3I6aYf8YfD8zltermCTe6Qhl61gnVg0ZvYorpDp7gE84BAAAOAQAAEpQ.jpg?imageView2/1/w/555/h/555\" />\n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>2018年的英仙座流星雨，这是整晚的流星叠加在一张图上的效果 |&nbsp;高尚国 &amp;&nbsp;夜空中国</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>一年一度的英仙座流星雨，将在今晚（8月12日）达到极大。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p><span><strong>今年的这场流星雨，特别适合中国观赏 </strong> </span> ，因为对于我们所处的东亚地区来说，极大刚好落在今晚的前半夜，月亮尚未升起之时。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>如果能够离开城市的灯光，来到更为黑暗的郊外观赏，你每小时应该能够看到60颗以上的流星。</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section> \n     <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n      <section> \n       <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n        <p><span><strong><span>太长不看版： </span> </strong> </span></p> \n        <p>&nbsp;</p> \n        <ul class=\"list-paddingleft-2\"> \n         <li> <p><span>对于我国大部分地区来说，最佳观测时间是8月12日天黑之后到后半夜月升之前。 </span></p> </li> \n         <li> <p><span>找一片开阔地，躺下，仰望即可。不需要望远镜，直接用肉眼就好。 </span></p> </li> \n         <li> <p><span>平均而言，大约每分钟，你会看到一两颗流星在夜空中划过。 </span></p> </li> \n         <li> <p><span>流星出现的方位是随机的，但所有的英仙座流星看起来都像从东北方向的英仙座中辐射出来。</span></p> </li> \n        </ul> \n       </section> \n      </section> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>流星雨之所以出现，是因为地球环绕太阳的公转轨道上，多少散布着一些彗星（偶尔也有小行星）撒落的碎屑。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>彗星通常由尘埃和砂砾混和着水冰而构成，当它被太阳加热时，冰就会升华喷出，带出一些尘埃碎屑。这些碎屑沿着与彗星轨道相似的路线绕太阳公转。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>当地球从尘埃带中穿过时，它们就会高速闯入大气层，受热发光。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>于是，我们就有了一场流星雨。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p><img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"1.33125\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"640\" src=\"https://3-im.guokr.com/5rGthBD0QO4rgYzZaDVSdWDTarQn7KQ36b7YIdaN83-AAgAAVAMAAEpQ.jpg?imageView2/1/w/555/h/738\"><br> <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"1.221875\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"640\" src=\"https://3-im.guokr.com/xzEs4StXegQUe1yG8hqTzOWYnWDl-DyQqzS0EUz7VPqAAgAADgMAAEpQ.jpg?imageView2/1/w/555/h/678\"><br> <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"1.0546875\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"640\" src=\"https://3-im.guokr.com/YJlZVMQxvqGm8SlkLM594rma5VqDsd05U4gUe5doJzKAAgAAowIAAEpQ.jpg?imageView2/1/w/555/h/585\"><br> <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.978125\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"640\" src=\"https://2-im.guokr.com/pjRWGApewSi0r0d4XAgGV-7xCCUw1XcbHKJhYBqfkXmAAgAAcgIAAEpQ.jpg?imageView2/1/w/555/h/542\"><br> <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"1.0296875\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"640\" src=\"https://3-im.guokr.com/piwq1imdpifpfArBGRY2a-PMvaNaRBzndaUd5-jNW8GAAgAAkwIAAEpQ.jpg?imageView2/1/w/555/h/571\" /></br></img></br></img></br></img></br></img></p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>英仙座流星雨就是这样形成的 |&nbsp;EasyNight</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>英仙座流星雨就是斯威夫特－塔特尔彗星（comet Swift-Tuttle）撒落的碎屑与地球相遇的结果。这颗彗星每130年环绕太阳一圈。地球会在每年8月穿过这颗彗星的轨道。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>由于透视关系，这些流星看上去都是从天空中的一点射出的，这个辐射点就位于英仙座中，流星雨也因此而得名。</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section> \n     <section> \n      <p>什么时间看最好？</p> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>理论上说，英仙座流星雨从7月17号开始，一直持续到8月底。不过，值得欣赏的流星雨极大期，出现在8月12－13日前后。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p><span><strong>今年，最佳观测时间应该是8月12日夜晚 </strong> </span> 。前半夜，正赶上预报的极大值，并且完全没有月光干扰。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>到了后半夜，农历廿四的残月会从东方升起，给看流星带来一些干扰。不过，后半夜辐射点升高，流星出现的数量也会增多，算是各有利弊吧……</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>然而，毕竟不是周末，如果真想熬个通宵的话，第二天怕是没有精力好好搬砖了。</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section> \n     <section> \n      <p>能看到多少流星，</p> \n      <p>多久能看到一颗？</p> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>英仙座流星雨平均每小时出现大约60－100颗流星。通常人们能够看到的数量要少很多，因为大多数人头顶上的夜空都不是特别黑。流星是随机出现的， <span> <strong> 你有可能在几秒钟内接连看到三四颗，也可能在接下来的五六分钟里颗粒无收 </strong> </span> 。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>很多人有这样一个错误观念，认为流星雨像烟花一样，能够看到流星满天飞舞。真实情况不是这样，大约一分钟才能看到一颗。不过，这仍然足够震撼！</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>另外，别指望一来到户外就能马上看到大量流星。你的眼睛要花好几分钟才能适应黑暗，完全适应要花大约半个小时。所以，出门之后等上几分钟。要有耐心！</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section> \n     <section> \n      <p>应该朝哪个方向看？</p> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p><span><strong>向上看！ </strong> </span></p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>真的，流星可能出现在天空中的任何方位，所以你能看到的天空越多越好。试着避开建筑和树木，如果能够找地方仰躺下来就最好。</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section> \n     <section> \n      <p>需要夜空够黑暗吗？</p> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>避开城市灯光会很有帮助。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>许多流星都很暗，如果天空被光污染照亮，这些暗流星就会淹没在天光之中，看不到了。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>不过，就算是在城区，只要天气晴朗，避开耀眼的灯光，通常也能看到一些较亮的流星。当然，流星的数量会大打折扣。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section>\n     <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"1.4388715\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"638\" src=\"https://1-im.guokr.com/eIx2BXPO5Zz2JsoqJrPBPp0yAioQQp7IPUIw6FiMRxR-AgAAlgMAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/798\" />\n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section>\n     <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"1.6809623\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"956\" src=\"https://1-im.guokr.com/0Prlc6QA-i6cJ-PfMsSVY8tXy9hMT_QN04-8YwjDnZ68AwAARwYAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/932\" />\n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section>\n     <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.799373\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"957\" src=\"https://1-im.guokr.com/UWL13fmlRPJv-ZttlG2yYvCtO5fBS-4mIQ1hAe8bErS9AwAA_QIAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/443\" />\n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p><img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"1.853125\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"640\" src=\"https://1-im.guokr.com/OIgSZNEufsTTzV2hwXXzsLziXoua1ubwOHOnLA6BFlGAAgAAogQAAEpQ.jpg?imageView2/1/w/555/h/1028\"><br> <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"1.3890625\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"640\" src=\"https://1-im.guokr.com/6j8yzGxnjneA4Xg40dmXazke9Vp-8kw7NtSmh4klZc-AAgAAeQMAAEpQ.jpg?imageView2/1/w/555/h/770\"><br> <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"1.11875\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"640\" src=\"https://2-im.guokr.com/0WTtXS-hIAFqtjF5plO62sE6lAzBr_KLctK7VoXlX0uAAgAAzAIAAEpQ.jpg?imageView2/1/w/555/h/620\" /></br></img></br></img></p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>一张图告诉你英仙座流星雨要怎么看 | EasyNight</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section> \n     <section> \n      <p>要用望远镜或者双筒镜看吗？</p> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>流星可能出现在天空的任意方向，你需要留意尽可能多的天空，因此 <span> <strong> 肉眼是你看流星雨的最佳装备 </strong> </span> 。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>而望远镜只能让你一次看到一小片天空，很可能会错过所有的流星。这就好比你想要透过一根吸管，来看一场烟花汇演一样。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>不过，如果有双筒镜，不妨带去野外。虽然会让你错过一些流星，但花几分钟用双筒镜扫视夏夜银河，绝对值得一看。</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section> \n     <section> \n      <p>流星速度有多快？</p> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>典型的英仙座流星在进入地球大气层的时候，速度大约是60千米/秒，也就是每小时20万千米。这个速度非常快，只要2个小时就能从地球飞到月亮。</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section> \n     <section> \n      <p>这么快，那会不会被流星砸到？</p> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>不会。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>这些流星通常都不会比雪花或者沙粒大多少。它们在距离地面90－100千米的高空就会烧尽，不会掉落到你头上。</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section> \n     <section> \n      <p>宇航员会有危险吗？</p> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>不太会。国际空间站被击中的几率非常低。不过，2011年，宇航员罗恩·加兰拍到过一颗在他下方燃烧的英仙座流星。是不是很酷？</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section>\n     <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.5\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1024\" src=\"https://3-im.guokr.com/hdAGD-aVyhaK4YJfuUx8YVkdWIJQ3FiYhKHRCs1aMAQABAAAAAIAAEpQ.jpg?imageView2/1/w/555/h/277\" />\n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>宇航员可以在俯瞰地球的时候拍到英仙座流星，因为他们的位置比流星要高 | NASA</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section> \n     <section> \n      <p>为什么流星会拖尾？</p> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>那是气化的流星物质！随着流星体高速穿过空气，它会剧烈压缩前方的空气，从而变得炽热——就好像你给自行车打气时，气筒里的气体受到压缩就会发热一样。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>流星体上的部分颗粒融化并脱落下来（天文学家称之为“烧蚀”），形成了长长的流星尾迹，要花上几秒钟才会冷却变暗。</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section> \n     <section> \n      <p>特别亮的流星，有时能看到尾巴持续好几分钟，那是什么？</p> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>高速穿过空气时，流星体会承受超高的压力。它有可能四分五裂，而分裂的碎片会更迅速地燃烧殆尽。这可能导致流星发生一次或者多次闪光，其实就是爆炸。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>流星体的解体会产生大量电离粒子，有时候能够持续好几分钟，然后在高空风的作用下逐渐扭曲飘散。这很罕见，但非常壮观。</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section>\n     <img data-=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.5633333\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"300\" src=\"https://1-im.guokr.com/Gv-LPChEPYz_aCgNCAFd4TaPqTAqZiAtJRhLYKdJNDMsAQAAqQAAAEdJ.gif\" />\n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>这是一颗火流星持续了很久的余迹 | Steed &amp;&nbsp;夜空中国</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section> \n     <section> \n      <p>为什么有些流星尾巴长，</p> \n      <p>有些尾巴短？</p> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>流星的尾巴的长短，取决于流星相对于你的角度。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>如果流星直冲你而来，尾巴看上去就会很短。如果流星跟你的视线方向刚好垂直，尾巴看起来就会很长。</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <section> \n     <section> \n      <p>怎么许愿才最灵？</p> \n     </section> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>据说，看到流星划过的时候，把愿望在心里默念3遍，如果流星还没有消失，这个愿望就能够实现。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>当然，这不科学。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>事实上，大部分流星一闪而过的时间都很短，除了“哇”出一声以外，你根本来不及作出其他反应。</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p>如果非要对着流星许愿的话，有一个愿望是在流星雨期间最灵和最容易实现的，那就是——</p> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n    <p><span><strong>再来一颗！ </strong> </span></p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p>&nbsp;</p> \n   </section> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"> \n    <p><span>作者：艾麦乐 </span></p> \n    <p><span>手绘插图：EasyNight
